msg:Located in the new business and government district area, the hotel is conveniently situated.for business travellers. The airport is about 20 minutes by car and also around 20 minutes to Taiyuan South railway station. Parking is also available at this property. Around the hotel are many restaurants and shops along with the giant MixC shopping mall. 
The hotel boasts a range of high-quality amenities including a SPA, gym and excellent swimming pool. The downstairs restaurant is also excellent, especially the breakfast buffet, which has many options available. The rooms are well-appointed with modern furniture and comfortable beds. The rooms are large and offer plenty of space too. 
Staff are very helpful and attentive and also speak good English. Highly recommended and my favorite hotel In Taiyuan!

name:W‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçj‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚ÄçJ‚Äça‚Äçv‚Äçe‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçn

posted:Posted November 20, 2023
msg:At first, I really didn't understand why there was this in the room...

InterContinental is probably a relatively new hotel in Taiyuan. Seeing that everyone was complaining about the old Kempinski, I didn't dare to book it. Seeing that everyone had good reviews here, I decided to try it.

Compared with Kempinski and Wanda, the location of InterContinental may be a little bit away from the city center, but I guess there are often meetings around, and it's not far away, it's still quite convenient.

I left a very good impression when I checked in. Catherine Cheng is very nice, and I'll give you a refill~

The room is good overall, with good space and comfort, and the hotel facilities are relatively new, so it looks better.

There is a machine in the bedroom, and two bottles of mineral water are placed next to it. I didn't understand it at first, but later I realized that probably because Shanxi is too dry, the hotel thoughtfully equipped the room with a humidifier and prepared extra purified water for the humidifier. Later, I moved to other hotels. It really feels too dry without a humidifier hahahahahahaha.

The bathroom is spacious, with double sinks, a bathtub and a shower. The toiletries are from the blanche series byredo, and the scent is also very nice.

The hotel's gym is relatively small, but it has all the usual facilities, and drinking water is also available in the gym.

The overall experience is quite satisfactory, especially if you drive there, it is very convenient to stay here. Of course, if you care about being close to the subway station, the location here may be a little disadvantageous.
